        }
        mr-issue-page[issueClosed] {
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: nowrap;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <h2>Email display settings</h2>

        <p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>

        <p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Allocate an uninitialized heap space via kmalloc, and copy it to userspace. Kernel info leak.



<span class="line"><!---->Allocate an uninitialized heap space via kmalloc, and copy it to userspace. Kernel info leak.<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





static long cros_ec_chardev_ioctl_xcmd(struct cros_ec_dev *ec, void __user *arg)



<span class="line"><!---->static long cros_ec_chardev_ioctl_xcmd(struct cros_ec_dev *ec, void __user *arg)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





        struct cros_ec_command *s_cmd;



<span class="line"><!---->        struct cros_ec_command *s_cmd;<!----></span>



<br>





        struct cros_ec_command u_cmd;



<span class="line"><!---->        struct cros_ec_command u_cmd;<!----></span>



<br>





        long ret;



<span class="line"><!---->        long ret;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (copy_from_user(&u_cmd, arg, sizeof(u_cmd)))



<span class="line"><!---->        if (copy_from_user(&amp;u_cmd, arg, sizeof(u_cmd)))<!----></span>



<br>





                return -EFAULT;



<span class="line"><!---->                return -EFAULT;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (u_cmd.outsize > EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES ||



<span class="line"><!---->        if (u_cmd.outsize &gt; EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES ||<!----></span>



<br>





            u_cmd.insize > EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES)



<span class="line"><!---->            u_cmd.insize &gt; EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES)<!----></span>



<br>





                return -EINVAL;



<span class="line"><!---->                return -EINVAL;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        s_cmd = kmalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),



<span class="line"><!---->        s_cmd = kmalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),<!----></span>



<br>





                        GFP_KERNEL);    <------ kmalloc, uninitialized heap data



<span class="line"><!---->                        GFP_KERNEL);    &lt;------ kmalloc, uninitialized heap data<!----></span>



<br>





        if (!s_cmd)



<span class="line"><!---->        if (!s_cmd)<!----></span>



<br>





                return -ENOMEM;



<span class="line"><!---->                return -ENOMEM;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (copy_from_user(s_cmd, arg, sizeof(*s_cmd) + u_cmd.outsize)) {



<span class="line"><!---->        if (copy_from_user(s_cmd, arg, sizeof(*s_cmd) + u_cmd.outsize)) {<!----></span>



<br>





                ret = -EFAULT;



<span class="line"><!---->                ret = -EFAULT;<!----></span>



<br>





                goto exit;



<span class="line"><!---->                goto exit;<!----></span>



<br>





        }



<span class="line"><!---->        }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (u_cmd.outsize != s_cmd->outsize ||



<span class="line"><!---->        if (u_cmd.outsize != s_cmd-&gt;outsize ||<!----></span>



<br>





            u_cmd.insize != s_cmd->insize) {



<span class="line"><!---->            u_cmd.insize != s_cmd-&gt;insize) {<!----></span>



<br>





                ret = -EINVAL;



<span class="line"><!---->                ret = -EINVAL;<!----></span>



<br>





                goto exit;



<span class="line"><!---->                goto exit;<!----></span>



<br>





        }



<span class="line"><!---->        }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        s_cmd->command += ec->cmd_offset;



<span class="line"><!---->        s_cmd-&gt;command += ec-&gt;cmd_offset;<!----></span>



<br>





        ret = cros_ec_cmd_xfer(ec->ec_dev, s_cmd);



<span class="line"><!---->        ret = cros_ec_cmd_xfer(ec-&gt;ec_dev, s_cmd);<!----></span>



<br>





        /* Only copy data to userland if data was received. */



<span class="line"><!---->        /* Only copy data to userland if data was received. */<!----></span>



<br>





        if (ret < 0)



<span class="line"><!---->        if (ret &lt; 0)<!----></span>



<br>





                goto exit;



<span class="line"><!---->                goto exit;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        if (copy_to_user(arg, s_cmd, sizeof(*s_cmd) + s_cmd->insize))   <------ copy to userspace



<span class="line"><!---->        if (copy_to_user(arg, s_cmd, sizeof(*s_cmd) + s_cmd-&gt;insize))   &lt;------ copy to userspace<!----></span>



<br>





                ret = -EFAULT;



<span class="line"><!---->                ret = -EFAULT;<!----></span>



<br>





exit:



<span class="line"><!---->exit:<!----></span>



<br>





        kfree(s_cmd);



<span class="line"><!---->        kfree(s_cmd);<!----></span>



<br>





        return ret;



<span class="line"><!---->        return ret;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Chrome: 111.0.5563.71



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome: 111.0.5563.71<!----></span>



<br>





ChromeOS: 111.0.5563.71



<span class="line"><!---->ChromeOS: 111.0.5563.71<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Bisect:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/_/chromium/chromiumos/third_party/kernel/+/eda2e30c6684d67288edb841c6125d48c608a242



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/_/chromium/chromiumos/third_party/kernel/+/eda2e30c6684d67288edb841c6125d48c608a242"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/_/chromium/chromiumos/third_party/kernel/+/eda2e30c6684d67288edb841c6125d48c608a242<!----></a>

Patch:



<span class="line"><!---->Patch:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





diff --git a/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c b/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c



<span class="line"><!---->diff --git a/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c b/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c<!----></span>



<br>





index 0de7c255254e..d6de5a294128 100644



<span class="line"><!---->index 0de7c255254e..d6de5a294128 100644<!----></span>



<br>





--- a/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c



<span class="line"><!---->--- a/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c<!----></span>



<br>





+++ b/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c



<span class="line"><!---->+++ b/drivers/platform/chrome/cros_ec_chardev.c<!----></span>



<br>





@@ -284,7 +284,7 @@ static long cros_ec_chardev_ioctl_xcmd(struct cros_ec_dev *ec, void __user *arg)



<span class="line"><!---->@@ -284,7 +284,7 @@ static long cros_ec_chardev_ioctl_xcmd(struct cros_ec_dev *ec, void __user *arg)<!----></span>



<br>





            u_cmd.insize > EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES)



<span class="line"><!---->            u_cmd.insize &gt; EC_MAX_MSG_BYTES)<!----></span>



<br>





                return -EINVAL;



<span class="line"><!---->                return -EINVAL;<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>





-       s_cmd = kmalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),



<span class="line"><!---->-       s_cmd = kmalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),<!----></span>



<br>





+       s_cmd = kzalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),



<span class="line"><!---->+       s_cmd = kzalloc(sizeof(*s_cmd) + max(u_cmd.outsize, u_cmd.insize),<!----></span>



<br>





                        GFP_KERNEL);



<span class="line"><!---->                        GFP_KERNEL);<!----></span>



<br>





        if (!s_cmd)



<span class="line"><!---->        if (!s_cmd)<!----></span>



<br>





                return -ENOMEM;



<span class="line"><!---->                return -ENOMEM;<!----></span>

<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
